   (function(){
        var onTerminatedPageLoad = (function(){
            var callback = null;

            // We are going to detect if the user aborts the page load. Oh yes. This is fun.
            if ( document.onstop !== undefined )
            {
                // IE makes this easy, thanks IE.
                document.onstop = function()
                {
                    if ( callback != null )
                    {
                        callback();
                    }
                };
            }
            else
            {
                // Enter the realm of weirdness
                var hasSeenInteractive = false,
                        hasSeenComplete = false;

                document.addEventListener(
                        'readystatechange',
                        function()
                        {
                            var state = document.readyState;
                            if ( state === 'interactive' )
                            {
                                hasSeenInteractive = true;
                            }
                            else if ( state === 'complete' )
                            {
                                hasSeenComplete = true;

                                // Chrome sets readyState to `complete` before `interactive` if pageload is aborted.
                                if ( !hasSeenInteractive )
                                {
                                    if ( callback != null )
                                    {
                                        callback();
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                );

                window.addEventListener(
                        'pageshow',
                        function()
                        {
                            if ( !hasSeenComplete )
                            {
                                // Firefox doesn't set readyState to `complete` before firing onpageshow
                                if ( callback != null )
                                {
                                    callback();
                                }
                            }
                        }
                );
            }

            return function( the_callback )
            {
                callback = the_callback;
            }
        })();

        var jselLog = {},
            isPageTerminated = false,
            isPageLoaded = false,
            errorQueue = [],
            hashFunc = function( str ) {
                var hash = 0, i, l = str.length, chr;
                if ( l === 0 ) return hash;
                for ( i = 0; i &lt; l; i++ )
                {
                    chr = str.charCodeAt( i );
                    hash = ( ( hash &lt;&lt; 5 ) - hash ) + chr;
                    hash = hash &amp; hash;
                }
                return hash;
            },
            jselDetach = function()
            {
                isPageTerminated = true;
            };

        window.jselError = function( error )
        {
            if ( isPageTerminated )
            {
                // Pageload was terminated by user, we don't care about any of their errors
                return;
            }

            try {
                var blacklist = ["Script error", "Script error."];
                var errorMessage = (error &amp;&amp; error.message) ? error.message : (window &amp;&amp; window.event &amp;&amp; window.event.errorMessage) ? window.event.errorMessage : "Unknown message.";

                // Don't handle errors in blacklist.
                if ( blacklist.indexOf( errorMessage ) !== -1 ) { return false; }

                var fileName = (error &amp;&amp; error.filename) ? error.filename : "No file available.";
                var lineNumber = (error &amp;&amp; error.lineno !== undefined) ? error.lineno : (window &amp;&amp; window.event &amp;&amp; window.event.errorLine) ? window.event.errorLine : "Unknown error line.";
                var userAgent = (navigator &amp;&amp; navigator.userAgent) ? navigator.userAgent : "Unknown User Agent.";
                var payload = {
                    jsp_timestamp: 1436902381292,
                    clientIP: '199.30.80.113',
                    stacktrace: error.error ? error.error.stack || '' : ''
                };
                var eObject = {
                        error: errorMessage,
                        file: fileName,
                        line: lineNumber,
                        sessionId: 'C4D037601A32724ED93E23E62DDF0BEF.bowie001',
                        sympSessionId: '1436902380985:5ab9fsu8',
                        url: document.location.href,
                        userAgent: userAgent,
                        payload: payload
                    },
                    request = null;

                var hash = hashFunc( errorMessage );
                var count = jselLog[ hash ];
                var doLog = ( count !== -1 );

                if ( count === undefined )
                {
                    jselLog[ hash ] = 1;
                    doLog = true;
                }
                else if ( count !== -1 )
                {
                    ++count;
                    jselLog[ hash ] = count;
                }

                if ( count &gt;= 500 )
                {
                    jselLog[ hash ] = -1;
                    eObject.error += " THROTTLE HIT!";
                }

                if ( doLog )
                {
                    if ( window.XMLHttpRequest ) {
                        request = new XMLHttpRequest();
                    } else {
                        if ( window.ActiveXObject ) {
                            try {
                                request = new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
                            } catch( e ) {}
                        }
                    }
                    if ( request !== null ) {
                        request.open("POST", "http://jsel.sympoz.com:36606/", true);
                        request.setRequestHeader("Content-type", "application/json");
                        request.send( JSON.stringify( eObject ) );
                    }
                }
            }
            catch( e ) { if (window.console) { console.log( e ); } }
        };

        onTerminatedPageLoad( jselDetach );
        if ( navigator.userAgent.indexOf( 'Firefox' ) !== -1 )
        {
            window.onerror = function( message, file, line, col, error )
            {
                jselError({
                    message: message,
                    filename: file,
                    lineno: line,
                    error: error
                });
            };
            window.addEventListener( 'beforeunload', jselDetach );
        }
        else if ( window.addEventListener )
        {
            window.addEventListener( 'error', jselError );
            window.addEventListener( 'beforeunload', jselDetach );
        }
        else if ( window.attachEvent )
        {
            window.attachEvent('onerror', jselError);
            window.attachEvent( 'onbeforeunload', jselDetach );
        }
    })();

    (function(){
        var matchIE = navigator.userAgent.match(/(trident).+rv[:\s]((\d+)?[\w\.]+).+like\sgecko/i);
        if ( matchIE )
        {
            var majorVersion = matchIE[3];
            if ( majorVersion === '11' )

                isIE = true;

                isIEgt8 = true;

        }
    })();

    var isAndroid = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().indexOf( "android" ) != -1;
    var isSurface = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().indexOf( "touch" ) != -1;
    var isTablet = false;
    var isMobile = false &amp;&amp; !isTablet;
    //isiOS5 also tests for iOS 4 as well

    var isiOSLessThan6 = ( isiPhone || isiPad ) &amp;&amp; ( navigator.userAgent.indexOf( 'OS 5' ) !== -1 || navigator.userAgent.indexOf( 'OS 4' ) !== -1 );
    var isiOS7 = false;

    // This wonderful bit of code checks for IE10.
    /*@cc_on
     if (/^10/.test(@_jscript_version)) {
     isIE = true;
     isIE10 = true;
     ie = 'IE10';
     }
     @*/

    // Check for modern versions of IE via the user agent
    (function(){
        var matchIE = navigator.userAgent.match(/(trident).+rv[:\s]((\d+)?[\w\.]+).+like\sgecko/i);
        if ( matchIE )
        {
            var majorVersion = matchIE[3];
            if ( majorVersion === '11' )
            {
                isIE = true;
                isIEgte8 = true;
                isIEgt8 = true;
                isIEgte9 = true;
                isIE11 = true;
            }
        }
    })();


    var _userVideoSettings = '{"deliverySetting":"BEST_FIT","craftsyHelp":true,"bitrate":"HIGH"}';
    var _isProduction = true;
    var _userEmailMD5 = '';
    var isLoggedIn=false;
    var userId=0;
    if(!enrollableId){ var enrollableId=0; };
    var enroll={};
    if(!enrollRegType){var enrollRegType = '';}
    if(!paymentModal){var paymentModal='payment';}
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   var loadCSS = (function(){
        return function loadCSS( href, media, callback ) {
            "use strict";
            // Arguments explained:
            // `href` is the URL for your CSS file.
            // However, since the order in which stylesheets are referenced matters, you might need a more specific location in your document.
            // If so, pass a different reference element to the `before` argument and it'll insert before that instead
            var ss = window.document.createElement( "link" );
            var sheets = window.document.styleSheets;
            ss.rel = "stylesheet";
            ss.type = "text/css";
            ss.href = href;
            // temporarily, set media to something non-matching to ensure it'll fetch without blocking render
            ss.media = "only x";
            ss.onload = callback || function() {};
            // inject link
            document.head.appendChild( ss );
            // This function sets the link's media back to `all` so that the stylesheet applies once it loads
            // It is designed to poll until document.styleSheets includes the new sheet.
            function toggleMedia(){
                var defined;
                for( var i = 0; i &lt; sheets.length; i++ ){
                    if( sheets[ i ].href &amp;&amp; sheets[ i ].href.indexOf( href ) &gt; -1 ){
                        defined = true;
                    }
                }
                if( defined ){
                    ss.media = media || "all";
                }
                else {
                    setTimeout( toggleMedia );
                }
            }
            toggleMedia();
            return ss;
        };
    })();
  </script>

  <script>
   (function(i,s,o,g,r,a,m){i['GoogleAnalyticsObject']=r;i[r]=i[r]||function()
    { (i[r].q=i[r].q||[]).push(arguments)}
            ,i[r].l=1*new Date();a=s.createElement(o),
            m=s.getElementsByTagName(o)[0];a.async=1;a.src=g;m.parentNode.insertBefore(a,m)
    })(window,document,'script','//www.google-analytics.com/analytics.js','ga');

    ga('create', 'UA-22901171-1', 'craftsy.com');
    ga('create', 'UA-22901171-1',
            {'siteSpeedSampleRate': 3}
    );

    // Optimizely Universal Analytics Integration Code
    window.optimizely = window.optimizely || [];
    window.optimizely.push('activateUniversalAnalytics');
    // End Optimizely Code

    ga('require', 'displayfeatures');
    ga('send', 'pageview');

    // Track user interaction on the page
    // modified from http://cutroni.com/blog/2014/02/12/advanced-content-tracking-with-universal-analytics/
    (function() {
        if ( window.jQuery == null ) return;

        // Debug flag
        var debugMode = false;

        // Default time delay before checking location
        var callBackTime = 100;

        // # px before tracking a reader
        var readerLocation = 1000;

        // Set some flags for tracking &amp; execution
        var timer = 0;
        var scroller = false;
        var endContent = false;

        // Set some time variables to calculate reading time
        var startTime = new Date();
        var beginning = startTime.getTime();
        var amishTime = 0;

        // Get some information about the current page
        var pageTitle = document.title;

        // Check the location and track user
        function trackLocation() {
            bottom = $(window).height() + $(window).scrollTop();
            height = $(document).height();

            var scrollStart = new Date().getTime();

            // If user starts to scroll send an event
            if (bottom &gt; readerLocation &amp;&amp; !scroller) {
                timeToScroll = Math.round((scrollStart - beginning) / 1000);
                if (!debugMode) {
                    ga('send', 'event', 'Reading', 'StartReading', pageTitle, timeToScroll, {'metric1' : timeToScroll});
                } else {
                    console.log('started reading ' + timeToScroll);
                }
                scroller = true;
            }

            // If user has hit the bottom of the content send an event
            var $craftsyFooter = $('#craftsyFooter' );
            if ($craftsyFooter.length &gt; 0) {
                if (bottom &gt;= $craftsyFooter.position().top &amp;&amp; !endContent) {
                    contentScrollEnd = new Date().getTime();
                    timeToContentEnd = Math.round((contentScrollEnd - scrollStart) / 1000);
                    if (!debugMode) {
                        if (timeToContentEnd &lt; 60) {
                            ga('set', 'dimension5', 'Scanner');
                        } else {
                            ga('set', 'dimension5', 'Reader');
                        }
                        ga('send', 'event', 'Reading', 'ContentBottom', pageTitle, timeToContentEnd, {'nonInteraction': 1, 'metric2' : timeToContentEnd});
                    } else {
                        console.log('end content section '+timeToContentEnd);
                    }
                    endContent = true;
                }
            }
        }

        // Track the scrolling and track location
        $(window).scroll(function() {
            if (timer) {
                clearTimeout(timer);
            }

            // Use a buffer so we don't call trackLocation too often.
            timer = setTimeout(trackLocation, callBackTime);
        });
    })();
  </script>
